15/// The version of [Unicode](http://www.unicode.org/)
16/// that this version of unicode-segmentation is based on.
17pub const UNICODE_VERSION: (u64, u64, u64) = (16, 0, 0);
18
19const UNICODE_VERSION_U8: (u8, u8, u8) = (16, 0, 0);
20
21pub mod util {
22    #[inline]
23    pub fn bsearch_range_table(c: char, r: &[(char,char)]) -> bool {
24        use core::cmp::Ordering::{Equal, Less, Greater};
25        r.binary_search_by(|&(lo,hi)| {
26            if lo <= c && c <= hi { Equal }
27            else if hi < c { Less }
28            else { Greater }
29        }).is_ok()
30    }
31
32    #[inline]
33    fn is_alphabetic(c: char) -> bool {
34        if super::UNICODE_VERSION_U8 == char::UNICODE_VERSION {
35            c.is_alphabetic()
36        } else {
37            match c {
38                'a' ..= 'z' | 'A' ..= 'Z' => true,
39                c if c > '\x7f' => super::derived_property::Alphabetic(c),
40                _ => false,
41            }
42        }
43    }
44
45    #[inline]
46    fn is_numeric(c: char) -> bool {
47        if super::UNICODE_VERSION_U8 == char::UNICODE_VERSION {
48            c.is_numeric()
49        } else {
50            match c {
51                '0' ..= '9' => true,
52                c if c > '\x7f' => super::general_category::N(c),
53                _ => false,
54            }
55        }
56    }
57
58    #[inline]
59    pub fn is_alphanumeric(c: char) -> bool {
60        is_alphabetic(c) || is_numeric(c)
61    }
62}

484
485pub fn is_incb_linker(c: char) -> bool {
486    matches!(c, | '\u{94D}' | '\u{9CD}' | '\u{ACD}' | '\u{B4D}' | '\u{C4D}' | '\u{D4D}')
487}
488
489pub mod grapheme {
490    use core::result::Result::{Ok, Err};
491
492    pub use self::GraphemeCat::*;
493
494    #[allow(non_camel_case_types)]
495    #[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Debug)]
496    pub enum GraphemeCat {
497        GC_Any,
498        GC_CR,
499        GC_Control,
500        GC_Extend,
501        GC_Extended_Pictographic,
502        GC_InCB_Consonant,
503        GC_L,
504        GC_LF,
505        GC_LV,
506        GC_LVT,
507        GC_Prepend,
508        GC_Regional_Indicator,
509        GC_SpacingMark,
510        GC_T,
511        GC_V,
512        GC_ZWJ,
513    }
514
515    fn bsearch_range_value_table(c: char, r: &[(char, char, GraphemeCat)], default_lower: u32, default_upper: u32) -> (u32, u32, GraphemeCat) {
516        use core::cmp::Ordering::{Equal, Less, Greater};
517        match r.binary_search_by(|&(lo, hi, _)| {
518            if lo <= c && c <= hi { Equal }
519            else if hi < c { Less }
520            else { Greater }
521        }) {
522            Ok(idx) => {
523                let (lower, upper, cat) = r[idx];
524                (lower as u32, upper as u32, cat)
525            }
526            Err(idx) => {
527                (
528                    if idx > 0 { r[idx-1].1 as u32 + 1 } else { default_lower },
529                    r.get(idx).map(|c|c.0 as u32 - 1).unwrap_or(default_upper),
530                    GC_Any,
531                )
532            }
533        }
534    }
535
536    pub fn grapheme_category(c: char) -> (u32, u32, GraphemeCat) {
537        // Perform a quick O(1) lookup in a precomputed table to determine
538        // the slice of the range table to search in.
539        let lookup_interval = 0x80;
540        let idx = (c as u32 / lookup_interval) as usize;
541        let range = grapheme_cat_lookup.get(idx..(idx + 2)).map_or(
542          // If the `idx` is outside of the precomputed table - use the slice
543          // starting from the last covered index in the precomputed table and
544          // ending with the length of the range table.
545          1474..1480,
546          |r| (r[0] as usize)..((r[1] + 1) as usize)
547        );
548
549        // Compute pessimistic default lower and upper bounds on the category.
550        // If character doesn't map to any range and there is no adjacent range
551        // in the table slice - these bounds has to apply.
552        let lower = idx as u32 * lookup_interval;
553        let upper = lower + lookup_interval - 1;
554        bsearch_range_value_table(c, &grapheme_cat_table[range], lower, upper)
555    }

1246
1247pub mod word {
1248    use core::result::Result::{Ok, Err};
1249
1250    pub use self::WordCat::*;
1251
1252    #[allow(non_camel_case_types)]
1253    #[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Debug)]
1254    pub enum WordCat {
1255        WC_ALetter,
1256        WC_Any,
1257        WC_CR,
1258        WC_Double_Quote,
1259        WC_Extend,
1260        WC_ExtendNumLet,
1261        WC_Format,
1262        WC_Hebrew_Letter,
1263        WC_Katakana,
1264        WC_LF,
1265        WC_MidLetter,
1266        WC_MidNum,
1267        WC_MidNumLet,
1268        WC_Newline,
1269        WC_Numeric,
1270        WC_Regional_Indicator,
1271        WC_Single_Quote,
1272        WC_WSegSpace,
1273        WC_ZWJ,
1274    }
1275
1276    fn bsearch_range_value_table(c: char, r: &[(char, char, WordCat)], default_lower: u32, default_upper: u32) -> (u32, u32, WordCat) {
1277        use core::cmp::Ordering::{Equal, Less, Greater};
1278        match r.binary_search_by(|&(lo, hi, _)| {
1279            if lo <= c && c <= hi { Equal }
1280            else if hi < c { Less }
1281            else { Greater }
1282        }) {
1283            Ok(idx) => {
1284                let (lower, upper, cat) = r[idx];
1285                (lower as u32, upper as u32, cat)
1286            }
1287            Err(idx) => {
1288                (
1289                    if idx > 0 { r[idx-1].1 as u32 + 1 } else { default_lower },
1290                    r.get(idx).map(|c|c.0 as u32 - 1).unwrap_or(default_upper),
1291                    WC_Any,
1292                )
1293            }
1294        }
1295    }
1296
1297    pub fn word_category(c: char) -> (u32, u32, WordCat) {
1298        // Perform a quick O(1) lookup in a precomputed table to determine
1299        // the slice of the range table to search in.
1300        let lookup_interval = 0x80;
1301        let idx = (c as u32 / lookup_interval) as usize;
1302        let range = word_cat_lookup.get(idx..(idx + 2)).map_or(
1303          // If the `idx` is outside of the precomputed table - use the slice
1304          // starting from the last covered index in the precomputed table and
1305          // ending with the length of the range table.
1306          1082..1085,
1307          |r| (r[0] as usize)..((r[1] + 1) as usize)
1308        );
1309
1310        // Compute pessimistic default lower and upper bounds on the category.
1311        // If character doesn't map to any range and there is no adjacent range
1312        // in the table slice - these bounds has to apply.
1313        let lower = idx as u32 * lookup_interval;
1314        let upper = lower + lookup_interval - 1;
1315        bsearch_range_value_table(c, &word_cat_table[range], lower, upper)
1316    }
1317

1858pub mod emoji {
1859    use core::result::Result::{Ok, Err};
1860
1861    pub use self::EmojiCat::*;
1862
1863    #[allow(non_camel_case_types)]
1864    #[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Debug)]
1865    pub enum EmojiCat {
1866        EC_Any,
1867        EC_Extended_Pictographic,
1868    }
1869
1870    fn bsearch_range_value_table(c: char, r: &[(char, char, EmojiCat)], default_lower: u32, default_upper: u32) -> (u32, u32, EmojiCat) {
1871        use core::cmp::Ordering::{Equal, Less, Greater};
1872        match r.binary_search_by(|&(lo, hi, _)| {
1873            if lo <= c && c <= hi { Equal }
1874            else if hi < c { Less }
1875            else { Greater }
1876        }) {
1877            Ok(idx) => {
1878                let (lower, upper, cat) = r[idx];
1879                (lower as u32, upper as u32, cat)
1880            }
1881            Err(idx) => {
1882                (
1883                    if idx > 0 { r[idx-1].1 as u32 + 1 } else { default_lower },
1884                    r.get(idx).map(|c|c.0 as u32 - 1).unwrap_or(default_upper),
1885                    EC_Any,
1886                )
1887            }
1888        }
1889    }
1890
1891    pub fn emoji_category(c: char) -> (u32, u32, EmojiCat) {
1892        // Perform a quick O(1) lookup in a precomputed table to determine
1893        // the slice of the range table to search in.
1894        let lookup_interval = 0x80;
1895        let idx = (c as u32 / lookup_interval) as usize;
1896        let range = emoji_cat_lookup.get(idx..(idx + 2)).map_or(
1897          // If the `idx` is outside of the precomputed table - use the slice
1898          // starting from the last covered index in the precomputed table and
1899          // ending with the length of the range table.
1900          77..78,
1901          |r| (r[0] as usize)..((r[1] + 1) as usize)
1902        );
1903
1904        // Compute pessimistic default lower and upper bounds on the category.
1905        // If character doesn't map to any range and there is no adjacent range
1906        // in the table slice - these bounds has to apply.
1907        let lower = idx as u32 * lookup_interval;
1908        let upper = lower + lookup_interval - 1;
1909        bsearch_range_value_table(c, &emoji_cat_table[range], lower, upper)
1910    }
1911

2012pub mod sentence {
2013    use core::result::Result::{Ok, Err};
2014
2015    pub use self::SentenceCat::*;
2016
2017    #[allow(non_camel_case_types)]
2018    #[derive(Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Debug)]
2019    pub enum SentenceCat {
2020        SC_ATerm,
2021        SC_Any,
2022        SC_CR,
2023        SC_Close,
2024        SC_Extend,
2025        SC_Format,
2026        SC_LF,
2027        SC_Lower,
2028        SC_Numeric,
2029        SC_OLetter,
2030        SC_SContinue,
2031        SC_STerm,
2032        SC_Sep,
2033        SC_Sp,
2034        SC_Upper,
2035    }
2036
2037    fn bsearch_range_value_table(c: char, r: &[(char, char, SentenceCat)], default_lower: u32, default_upper: u32) -> (u32, u32, SentenceCat) {
2038        use core::cmp::Ordering::{Equal, Less, Greater};
2039        match r.binary_search_by(|&(lo, hi, _)| {
2040            if lo <= c && c <= hi { Equal }
2041            else if hi < c { Less }
2042            else { Greater }
2043        }) {
2044            Ok(idx) => {
2045                let (lower, upper, cat) = r[idx];
2046                (lower as u32, upper as u32, cat)
2047            }
2048            Err(idx) => {
2049                (
2050                    if idx > 0 { r[idx-1].1 as u32 + 1 } else { default_lower },
2051                    r.get(idx).map(|c|c.0 as u32 - 1).unwrap_or(default_upper),
2052                    SC_Any,
2053                )
2054            }
2055        }
2056    }
2057
2058    pub fn sentence_category(c: char) -> (u32, u32, SentenceCat) {
2059        // Perform a quick O(1) lookup in a precomputed table to determine
2060        // the slice of the range table to search in.
2061        let lookup_interval = 0x80;
2062        let idx = (c as u32 / lookup_interval) as usize;
2063        let range = sentence_cat_lookup.get(idx..(idx + 2)).map_or(
2064          // If the `idx` is outside of the precomputed table - use the slice
2065          // starting from the last covered index in the precomputed table and
2066          // ending with the length of the range table.
2067          2462..2474,
2068          |r| (r[0] as usize)..((r[1] + 1) as usize)
2069        );
2070
2071        // Compute pessimistic default lower and upper bounds on the category.
2072        // If character doesn't map to any range and there is no adjacent range
2073        // in the table slice - these bounds has to apply.
2074        let lower = idx as u32 * lookup_interval;
2075        let upper = lower + lookup_interval - 1;
2076        bsearch_range_value_table(c, &sentence_cat_table[range], lower, upper)
2077    }
